# Text Elements
consider a Boeing 747 airliner cruising at a velocity of 550mi/h at 
a standard altitude of 38000ft, where the freestream pressure and 
the temperature are 432.6      and 390° R respectively. A one -fiftieth
scale model of it is tested in a wind tunnel where the temperature is 430 R.
Calculate the required velocity and pressure of the test airstream in the wind
tunnel such that the lift and drag coefficient measured for the wind-tunnel
model are the same as for free flight. Assume that both   and a are 
proportional to  ^dqwHw4b0

Note the Rankine (°R) is an absolute unit of temperature -> 0°Ra is the same as 0K but the change
of 1 R is the change of 1  F (Fahrenheit) and not 1 °C (Celsius) ^JH6Ka4w5

solution:  ^TECjg9aA

[[📘ClassNotes/👨‍🔧Mechanics/🌊Thermal and Fluid dynamics/✈️Aerodynamics/♎Important Conclusions and Lists/Important Variables and Numbers]] ^gSMscj8R

https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3SLrLpyNh8U ^MMMtjlWC

so we learned from this case that the wind-tunnel stream 
must be pressurized in order to simulate the proper free-
flight Reynolds number.  ^GyDFqfCD

f05c7fe10e3e0b3a85460e10ca760ccfdaa3edc5: $$^{\circ}$$
d7c60322ba39914739267a36594821693ff1cf24: $$^{\circ}$$
f903b73a73011566225669f5f8d65beef0515441: $$\mu$$

e94333fe8b1daf74aaa5d1816fb9a888149e2cb8: $$T^{\frac{1}{2}}$$
